
"-- Table: BOOK1
======================================================

  CREATE TABLE "VORSCHRIFTEN_ADMIN"."BOOK1" 
   (	"ID" NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT ON NULL AS IDENTITY MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 120 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"B_NR_" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"CLUSTER__AUDI_VERTRIEB_BEGRIFF_" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"LAND__REGINDEX_BEGRIFF_" VARCHAR2(255), 
	"PRAXIS___RÜCKMELDUNG_IMPORTEUR" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"PRODUKTION_ZP8" VARCHAR2(255), 
	"HAFEN_EINGANG" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"HAFEN_AUSGANG" VARCHAR2(255), 
	"KENNZEICHENZUTEILUNG" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"BEMERKUNG" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"COL010" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"COL011" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"COL012" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"COL013" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"COL014" VARCHAR2(4000), 
	"BEDEUTUNG_EINSATZTERMIN" CLOB, 
	 PRIMARY KEY ("ID")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "VORSCHRIFTEN_DAT_OBJ"  ENABLE
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)

  CREATE TABLE "VORSCHRIFTEN_ADMIN"."ZZ_SUCHE_ALT" 
   (	"SUCHEID" NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT ON NULL AS IDENTITY MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 982 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"BEZEICHNUNG" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"BESCHREIBUNG" VARCHAR2(250),

	 CONSTRAINT "PK_SUCHE" PRIMARY KEY ("SUCHEID")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1

  TABLESPACE "VORSCHRIFTEN_DAT_OBJ"  ENABLE
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE

 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
